KB\n\n\ndef _embed_inputs(input_paths: list[Path]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Read input files and return their contents as fenced code blocks.\n\n    Each file is wrapped in a fenced block with a ``# <path>`` header.\n    Returns an empty string when *input_paths* is empty (no-op).\n    \"\"\"\n    if not input_paths:\n        return \"\"\n\n    blocks: list[str] = []\n    for p in input_paths:\n        content = Path(p).read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n        blocks.append(f\"# {p}\\n```\\n{content}\\n```\")\n    return \"\\n\\n\".join(blocks)\n\n\ndef _sanitize_output(output_file: Path) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Strip conversational preamble before YAML frontmatter in a step output file.\n\n    Reads the file, finds the first ``^---`` line, and removes everything before\n    it.  Uses atomic write (write to ``.tmp`` then ``os.replace()``) to prevent\n    partial file states.\n\n    Returns the byte count of the stripped preamble (0 when file already starts\n    with ``---`` or no frontmatter delimiter is found).\n    \"\"\"\n    import os\n    import re\n\n    try:\n        content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    except FileNotFoundError:\n        return 0\n\n    # Already starts with frontmatter delimiter -- nothing to strip\n    if content.lstrip().startswith(\"---\"):\n        return 0\n\n    # Search for the first ^--- line\n    match = re.search(r\"^---[ \\t]*$\", content, re.MULTILINE)\n    if match is None:\n        # No frontmatter found at all -- leave file unchanged\n        return 0\n\n    preamble = content[: match.start()]\n    cleaned = content[match.start() :]\n    preamble_bytes = len(preamble.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n\n    # Atomic write: tmp file + os.replace\n    tmp_file = output_file.with_suffix(output_file.suffix + \".tmp\")\n    tmp_file.write_text(cleaned, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    os.replace(tmp_file, output_file)\n\n    _log.info(\"Stripped %d-byte preamble from %s\", preamble_bytes, output_file)\n    return preamble_bytes\n\n\ndef _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(\n    output_file: Path,\n    started_at: datetime,\n    finished_at: datetime,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Inject executor-populated pipeline_diagnostics into extraction frontmatter.\n\n    The LLM cannot reliably produce execution timing or environment metadata,\n    so the executor injects these fields post-subprocess (FR-033).\n    \"\"\"\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n        return\n\n    # Find end of frontmatter\n    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", 3)\n    if end_idx == -1:\n        return\n\n    elapsed = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n    diagnostics_line = (\n        f\"pipeline_diagnostics: \"\n        f\"{{elapsed_seconds: {elapsed:.1f}, \"\n        f\"started_at: \\\"{started_at.isoformat()}\\\", \"\n        f\"finished_at: \\\"{finished_at.isoformat()}\\\"}}\"\n    )\n\n    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n    if embedded and len(embedded.encode(\"utf-8\")) <= _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n        extra_args: list[str] = []\n    elif embedded:\n        _log.warning(\n            \"Step '%s': embedded inputs exceed %d bytes, falling back to --file flags\",\n            step.id,\n            _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n        )\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = [\n            arg\n            for input_path in step.inputs\n            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n        ]\n    else:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = []\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n        prompt=effective_prompt,\n        output_file=step.output_file,\n        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=step.model or config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n        output_format=\"text\",\n        extra_args=extra_args,\n    )\n\n    proc.start()\n\n    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n        if cancel_check():\n            proc.terminate()\n            return StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=1,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n            )\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n    exit_code = proc.wait()\n    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    # Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\n    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n\n    # Inject executor-populated fields into extract step frontmatter (FR-033)\n    if step.id == \"extract\" and step.output_file.exists():\n        _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(step.output_file, started_at, finished_at)\n\n    # Process completed successfully; gate check happens in execute_pipeline\n    return StepResult(\n        step=step,\n        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n        attempt=1,\n        started_at=started_at,\n        finished_at=finished_at,\n    )\n\n\ndef build_certify_step(\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    findings: list | None = None,\n    context_sections: dict[str, str] | None = None,\n) -> Step:\n    \"\"\"Build a certify Step for execution via execute_pipeline().\n\n    The certify step runs as a standard Step (not ClaudeProcess directly)\n    per spec section 2.5. \"\"\"Format HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n    failed = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    passed = [r for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.PASS]\n    cancelled = [r for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.CANCELLED]\n\n    if not failed:\n        return \"\"\n\n    fail = failed[-1]\n    step = fail.step\n\n    # Calculate None,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Write .roadmap-state.json to output_dir via atomic tmp + os.replace().\n\n    Preserves existing ``validation``, ``fidelity_status``, ``remediate``,\n    and ``certify`` derive_pipeline_status(state: dict) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Derive the overall pipeline status from state transitions.\n\n    State transitions at each boundary:\n    - post-validate: validated | validated-with-issues\n    - post-remediate: remediated\n    - post-certify: certified | certified-with-caveats\n\n    Returns one of: 'pending', 'validated', 'validated-with-issues',\n    'remediated', 'certified', 'certified-with-caveats'.\n    \"\"\"\n    certify = state.get(\"certify\")\n    if certify is not None:\n        if certify.get(\"certified\", False):\n            return         return \"validated-with-issues\"\n\n    return \"pending\"\n\n\ndef write_state(state: dict, path: Path) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Write state dict to path atomically via tmp file + os.replace().\"\"\"\n    import os as _os\n\n    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    tmp = path.with_suffix(\".tmp\")\n    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(state, indent=2), if not path.exists():\n        return None\n    try:\n        text = path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n        if not text.strip():\n            return None\n        return json.loads(text)\n    except (json.JSONDecodeError, OSError):\n        return None\n\n\ndef apply_decomposition_pass(deliverables: list[Deliverable]) -> list[Deliverable]:\n    \"\"\"Post-generation decomposition pass for = False,\n    auto_accept: bool = False,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Execute the roadmap generation pipeline.\n\n    Builds the step list, handles --dry-run and --resume, then\n    delegates to execute_pipeline() with roadmap_run_step.\n\n    After all 9 steps pass, auto-invokes validation unless\n    --no-validate is set or --resume halted on a failed step.\n\n    Note: --no-validate does NOT skip the spec-fidelity step\n    (FR-010, AC-005). It only skips the post-pipeline validation\n    subsystem.\n\n    Args:\n        auto_accept: When True, the spec-patch resume cycle skips the\n            interactive prompt and proceeds automatically if evidence is\n            found. When False (default), the cycle prompts the user.\n            This is an internal parameter, not exposed on the CLI.\n    \"\"\"\n    config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.11: Recursion guard — local variable, per-invocation\n    _spec_patch_cycle_count = 0\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 3: Capture spec hash at function entry\n    initial_spec_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n\n    steps = _build_steps(config)\n\n    # --dry-run: print plan and exit\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _dry_run_output(steps)\n        return\n\n    # --resume: check which steps already pass their gates\n    if resume:\n        from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n\n        steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n\n    # Execute pipeline\n    results = execute_pipeline(\n        steps=steps,\n        config=config,\n        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n    )\n\n    # Save state\n    _save_state(config, results)\n\n    # Check for failures\n    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    if failures:\n        # FR-2.24.1.9: Check if spec-fidelity failed and auto-resume is possible\n        spec_fidelity_failed = any(\n            r.step and r.step.id == \"spec-fidelity\"\n            and r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)\n            for r in results\n        )\n\n        if spec_fidelity_failed:\n            resumed = _apply_resume_after_spec_patch(\n                config=config,\n                results=results,\n                auto_accept=auto_accept,\n                initial_spec_hash=initial_spec_hash,\n                cycle_count=_spec_patch_cycle_count,\n            )\n            if resumed:\n                _spec_patch_cycle_count += 1\n                # Cycle complete — resumed pipeline ran to completion or failure\n                # inside _apply_resume_after_spec_patch. If it returned True,\n                # we're done (either success or failure was handled internally).\n                return\n\n        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(results, config)\n        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    print(f\"\\n[roadmap] Pipeline complete: {len(results)} steps passed\", flush=True)\n\n    # Auto-invoke validation after successful pipeline completion\n    if no_validate:\n        print(\"[roadmap] Validation skipped (--no-validate)\", flush=True)\n        _save_validation_status(config, \"skipped\")\n        return\n\n    # Check if validation already completed (--resume path)\n    if resume:\n        state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n        state = read_state(state_file)\n        if state and \"validation\" in state:\n            saved = state[\"validation\"]\n            if saved.get(\"status\") in (\"pass\", \"fail\"):\n                print(\n                    f\"[roadmap] Validation already completed ({saved['status']}), skipping\",\n                    flush=True,\n                )\n                return\n\n    _auto_invoke_validate(config)\n\n\n\ndef _find_qualifying_deviation_files(\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    results: list[StepResult],\n) -> list:\n    \"\"\"Find deviation files written after spec-fidelity started.\n\n    Returns qualifying DeviationRecord objects, or empty list if\n    conditions are not met.\n\n    Implementation detail — not specified in the spec. Extracted for\n    testability of the three-condition detection gate.\n    \"\"\"\n    from .spec_patch import scan_accepted_deviation_records\n\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n    state = read_state(state_file)\n    if state is None:\n        return []\n\n    # Get spec-fidelity started_at timestamp\n    steps_state = state.get(\"steps\", {})\n    fidelity_state = steps_state.get(\"spec-fidelity\", {})\n    started_at_str = fidelity_state.get(\"started_at\")\n\n    # Fail-closed: if started_at is absent, condition not met\n    if not started_at_str:\n        return []\n\n    try:\n        started_at_ts = datetime.fromisoformat(started_at_str).timestamp()\n    except (ValueError, TypeError):\n        return []\n\n    # Scan all deviation records\n    all_records = scan_accepted_deviation_records(config.output_dir)\n    if not all_records:\n        return []\n\n    # Filter to records written AFTER spec-fidelity started (strict >)\n    qualifying = [r for r in all_records if r.mtime > started_at_ts]\n    return qualifying\n\n\ndef _apply_resume_after_spec_patch(\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    results: list[StepResult],\n    auto_accept: bool,\n    initial_spec_hash: str,\n    cycle_count: int,\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Attempt a single spec-patch auto-resume cycle after spec-fidelity FAIL.\n\n    Evaluates the three-condition detection gate (FR-2.24.1.9):\n      1. Recursion guard: cycle_count == 0\n      2. Qualifying deviation files exist with mtime > started_at\n      3. Spec file hash changed since run started (initial_spec_hash)\n\n    If all conditions pass, executes the six-step disk-reread sequence\n    (FR-2.24.1.10) and re-runs the pipeline via _apply_resume.\n\n    Single-writer assumption: no concurrent writer modifies\n    .roadmap-state.json between the reread and write steps.\n\n    Returns True if the cycle was attempted (regardless of outcome),\n    False if conditions were not met.\n    \"\"\"\n    # FR-2.24.1.11: Recursion guard\n    if cycle_count >= 1:\n        print(\n            \"[roadmap] Spec-patch cycle already exhausted \"\n            f\"(cycle_count={cycle_count}). Proceeding to normal failure.\",\n            flush=True,\n        )\n        return False\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 2: Qualifying deviation files\n    qualifying = _find_qualifying_deviation_files(config, results)\n    if not qualifying:\n        return False\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 3: Spec hash changed since run started\n    current_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n    if current_hash == initial_spec_hash:\n        return False\n\n    # All three conditions met — enter the cycle\n    # FR-2.24.1.12: Cycle entry logging\n    print(\n        f\"[roadmap] Spec patched by subprocess. \"\n        f\"Found {len(qualifying)} accepted deviation record(s).\",\n        flush=True,\n    )\n    print(\n        \"[roadmap] Triggering spec-hash sync and resume (cycle 1/1).\",\n        flush=True,\n    )\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.10: Six-step disk-reread sequence\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n\n    # Step 1: Re-read state from disk\n    _fresh_state = read_state(state_file)  # noqa: F841\n\n    # Step 2: Recompute spec hash\n    new_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n\n    # Step 3: Atomic write of new hash\n    try:\n        # Read again for fresh copy, update only spec_hash, write atomically\n        fresh_for_write = read_state(state_file) or {}\n        fresh_for_write[\"spec_hash\"] = new_hash\n        write_state(fresh_for_write, state_file)\n    except OSError as exc:\n        print(\n            f\"[roadmap] ERROR: Failed to update spec_hash during \"\n            f\"auto-resume cycle: {exc}. Falling through to normal failure.\",\n            file=sys.stderr,\n            flush=True,\n        )\n        return True  # Cycle was attempted but failed — don't retry\n\n    # Step 4: Re-read state from disk AGAIN (this is what _apply_resume gets)\n    post_write_state = read_state(state_file)\n    if post_write_state is None:\n        print(\n            \"[roadmap] ERROR: Could not re-read state after write. \"\n            \"Falling through to normal failure.\",\n            file=sys.stderr,\n            flush=True,\n        )\n        return True\n\n    # Step 5: Rebuild steps\n    steps = _build_steps(config)\n\n    # Step 6: Apply resume with post-write state\n    from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n\n    steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n\n    # Re-execute pipeline from the resumed point\n    resumed_results = execute_pipeline(\n        steps=steps,\n        config=config,\n        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n    )\n\n    # Save state from resumed run\n    _save_state(config, resumed_results)\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.12: Cycle completion logging\n    print(\"[roadmap] Spec-patch resume cycle complete.\", flush=True)\n\n    # Check if resumed pipeline also failed\n    resumed_failures = [\n        r for r in resumed_results\n        if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)\n    ]\n    if resumed_failures:\n        # Force re-run of extract on stale spec\n            if force_extract and entry.id == \"extract\":\n                found_failure = True\n                result.append(entry)\n                continue\n\n            if entry.gate:\n                passed, _reason = gate_fn(entry.output_file, entry.gate)\n                if passed:\n                    skipped += 1\n                    print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping {entry.id} (gate passes)\", flush=True)\n                    continue\n            found_failure = True\n            result.append(entry)\n\n    if skipped > 0:\n        print(f\"[roadmap] Skipped {skipped} steps (gates pass)\", flush=True)\n\n    if not result:\n        print(\"[roadmap] All steps already pass gates. Nothing to do.\", flush=True)\n\n    return result\n","numLines":1346,"startLine":1,"totalLines":1346}}}

Find end of frontmatter\n   129→    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", 3)\n   130→    if end_idx == -1:\n   131→        return\n   132→\n   133→    elapsed = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n   134→    diagnostics_line = (\n   135→        f\"pipeline_diagnostics: \"\n   136→        f\"{{elapsed_seconds: {elapsed:.1f}, \"\n   137→        f\"started_at: \\\"{started_at.isoformat()}\\\", \"\n   138→        f\"finished_at: \\\"{finished_at.isoformat()}\\\"}}\"\n   139→    )\n   140→\n   141→    # Insert before the closing ---\n   142→    new_content = (\n   143→        content[: end_idx]\n   144→        + \"\\n\"\n   145→        + diagnostics_line\n   146→        + content[end_idx:]\n   147→    )\n   148→    output_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   149→\n   150→\n   151→def roadmap_run_step(\n   152→    step: Step,\n   153→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   154→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n   155→) -> StepResult:\n   156→    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n   157→\n   158→    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n   159→    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n   160→    \"\"\"\n   161→    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   162→\n   163→    if config.dry_run:\n   164→        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n   165→        return StepResult(\n   166→            step=step,\n   167→            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   168→            attempt=1,\n   169→            started_at=started_at,\n   170→            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   171→        )\n   172→\n   173→    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n   174→    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n   175→    if embedded and len(embedded.encode(\"utf-8\")) <= _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n   176→        effective_prompt = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n   177→        extra_args: list[str] = []\n   178→    elif embedded:\n   179→        _log.warning(\n   180→            \"Step '%s': embedded inputs exceed %d bytes, falling back to --file flags\",\n   181→            step.id,\n   182→            _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n   183→        )\n   184→        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n   185→        extra_args = [\n   186→            arg\n   187→            for input_path in step.inputs\n   188→            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n   189→        ]\n   190→    else:\n   191→        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n   192→        extra_args = []\n   193→\n   194→    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n   195→        prompt=effective_prompt,\n   196→        output_file=step.output_file,\n   197→        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n   198→        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n   199→        model=step.model or config.model,\n   200→        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n   201→        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n   202→        output_format=\"text\",\n   203→        extra_args=extra_args,\n   204→    )\n   205→\n   206→    proc.start()\n   207→\n   208→    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n   209→    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n   210→        if cancel_check():\n   211→            proc.terminate()\n   212→            return StepResult(\n   213→                step=step,\n   214→                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n   215→                attempt=1,\n   216→                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n   217→                started_at=started_at,\n   218→                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   219→            )\n   220→        time.sleep(1)\n   221→\n   222→    exit_code = proc.wait()\n   223→    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   224→\n   225→    if exit_code == 124:\n   226→        return StepResult(\n   227→            step=step,\n   228→            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n   229→            attempt=1,\n   230→            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n   231→            started_at=started_at,\n   232→            finished_at=finished_at,\n   233→        )\n   234→\n   235→    if exit_code != 0:\n   236→        return StepResult(\n   237→            step=step,\n   238→            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n   239→            attempt=1,\n   240→            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n   241→            started_at=started_at,\n   242→            finished_at=finished_at,\n   243→        )\n   244→\n   245→    # Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\n   246→    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n   247→\n   248→    # Inject executor-populated fields into extract step frontmatter (FR-033)\n   249→    if step.id == \"extract\" and step.output_file.exists():\n   250→        _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(step.output_file, started_at, finished_at)\n   251→\n   252→    # Process completed successfully; gate check happens in execute_pipeline\n   253→    return StepResult(\n   254→        step=step,\n   255→        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   256→        attempt=1,\n   257→        started_at=started_at,\n   258→        finished_at=finished_at,\n   259→    )\n   260→\n   261→\n   262→def build_certify_step(\n   263→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n   264→    findings: list | None = None,\n   265→    context_sections: dict[str, str] | None = None,\n   266→) -> Step:\n   267→    \"\"\"Build a certify Step for execution via execute_pipeline().\n   268→\n   269→    The certify step runs as a standard Step (not ClaudeProcess directly)\n   270→    per spec section 2.5. 569→    results: list[StepResult],\n   570→    remediate_metadata: dict | None = None,\n   571→    certify_metadata: dict | None = None,\n   572→) -> None:\n   573→    \"\"\"Write .roadmap-state.json 699→\n   700→\n   701→def build_remediate_metadata(\n   702→    status: str,\n   703→    scope: str,\n   704→    findings_total: int,\n   705→    findings_actionable: int,\n   706→    findings_fixed: derive_pipeline_status(state: dict) -> str:\n   754→    \"\"\"Derive the overall pipeline status from state transitions.\n   755→\n   756→    State transitions at each boundary:\n   757→    - post-validate: validated | validated-with-issues\n   758→    - post-remediate: remediated\n   759→    - post-certify: certified | certified-with-caveats\n   760→\n   761→    Returns one of: 'pending', \"validated-with-issues\"\n   780→\n   781→    return \"pending\"\n   782→\n   783→\n   784→def write_state(state: dict, path: Path) -> None:\n   785→    \"\"\"Write state dict to path atomically via 804→        return None\n   805→\n   806→\n   807→def apply_decomposition_pass(deliverables: list[Deliverable]) -> list[Deliverable]:\n   808→    \"\"\"Post-generation decomposition pass for the roadmap pipeline.\n   809→\n   810→    Runs after deliverable generation, before output formatting.\n   811→    Splits behavioral deliverables into Implement/Verify pairs.\n   812→\n   813→ 822→def execute_roadmap(\n   823→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n   824→    resume: bool = False,\n   825→    no_validate: bool = False,\n   826→    auto_accept: bool = False,\n   827→) -> None:\n   828→    \"\"\"Execute the roadmap generation pipeline.\n   829→\n   830→    Builds the step list, handles --dry-run and --resume, then\n   831→    delegates to execute_pipeline() with roadmap_run_step.\n   832→\n   833→    After all 9 steps pass, auto-invokes validation unless\n   834→    --no-validate is set or --resume halted on a failed step.\n   835→\n   836→    Note: --no-validate does NOT skip the spec-fidelity step\n   837→    (FR-010, AC-005). It only skips the post-pipeline validation\n   838→    subsystem.\n   839→\n   840→    Args:\n   841→        auto_accept: When True, the spec-patch resume cycle skips the\n   842→            interactive prompt and proceeds automatically if evidence is\n   843→            found. When False (default), the cycle prompts the user.\n   844→            This is an internal parameter, not exposed on the CLI.\n   845→    \"\"\"\n   846→    config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   847→\n   848→    # FR-2.24.1.11: Recursion guard — local variable, per-invocation\n   849→    _spec_patch_cycle_count = 0\n   850→\n   851→    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 3: Capture spec hash at function entry\n   852→    initial_spec_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n   853→\n   854→    steps = _build_steps(config)\n   855→\n   856→    # --dry-run: print plan and exit\n   857→    if config.dry_run:\n   858→        _dry_run_output(steps)\n   859→        return\n   860→\n   861→    # --resume: check which steps already pass their gates\n   862→    if resume:\n   863→        from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n   864→\n   865→        steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n   866→\n   867→    # Execute pipeline\n   868→    results = execute_pipeline(\n   869→        steps=steps,\n   870→        config=config,\n   871→        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n   872→        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n   873→        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n   874→    )\n   875→\n   876→    # Save state\n   877→    _save_state(config, results)\n   878→\n   879→    # Check for failures\n   880→    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n   881→    if failures:\n   882→        # FR-2.24.1.9: Check if spec-fidelity failed and auto-resume is possible\n   883→        spec_fidelity_failed = any(\n   884→            r.step and r.step.id == \"spec-fidelity\"\n   885→            and r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)\n   886→            for r in results\n   887→        )\n   888→\n   889→        if spec_fidelity_failed:\n   890→            resumed = _apply_resume_after_spec_patch(\n   891→                config=config,\n   892→                results=results,\n   893→                auto_accept=auto_accept,\n   894→                initial_spec_hash=initial_spec_hash,\n   895→                cycle_count=_spec_patch_cycle_count,\n   896→            )\n   897→            if resumed:\n   898→                _spec_patch_cycle_count += 1\n   899→                # Cycle complete — resumed pipeline ran to completion or failure\n   900→                # inside _apply_resume_after_spec_patch. If it returned True,\n   901→                # we're done (either success or failure was handled internally).\n   902→                return\n   903→\n   904→        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(results, config)\n   905→        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n   906→        sys.exit(1)\n   907→\n   908→    print(f\"\\n[roadmap] Pipeline complete: {len(results)} steps passed\", flush=True)\n   909→\n   910→    # Auto-invoke validation after successful pipeline completion\n   911→    if no_validate:\n   912→        print(\"[roadmap] Validation skipped (--no-validate)\", flush=True)\n   913→        _save_validation_status(config, \"skipped\")\n   914→        return\n   915→\n   916→    # Check if validation already completed (--resume path)\n   917→    if resume:\n   918→        state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n   919→        state = read_state(state_file)\n   920→        if state and \"validation\" in state:\n   921→            saved = state[\"validation\"]\n   922→            if saved.get(\"status\") in (\"pass\", \"fail\"):\n   923→                print(\n   924→                    f\"[roadmap] Validation already completed ({saved['status']}), skipping\",\n   925→                    flush=True,\n   926→                )\n   927→                return\n   928→\n   929→    _auto_invoke_validate(config)\n   930→\n   931→\n   932→\n   933→def _find_qualifying_deviation_files(\n   934→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n   935→    results: list[StepResult],\n   936→) -> list:\n   937→    \"\"\"Find deviation files written after spec-fidelity started.\n   938→\n   939→    Returns qualifying DeviationRecord objects, or empty list if\n   940→    conditions are not met.\n   941→\n   942→    Implementation detail — not specified in the spec. Extracted for\n   943→    testability of the three-condition detection gate.\n   944→    \"\"\"\n   945→    from .spec_patch import scan_accepted_deviation_records\n   946→\n   947→    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n   948→    state = read_state(state_file)\n   949→    if state is None:\n   950→        return []\n   951→\n   952→    # Get spec-fidelity started_at timestamp\n   953→    steps_state = state.get(\"steps\", {})\n   954→    fidelity_state = steps_state.get(\"spec-fidelity\", {})\n   955→    started_at_str = fidelity_state.get(\"started_at\")\n   956→\n   957→    # Fail-closed: if started_at is absent, condition not met\n   958→    if not started_at_str:\n   959→        return []\n   960→\n   961→    try:\n   962→        started_at_ts = datetime.fromisoformat(started_at_str).timestamp()\n   963→    except (ValueError, TypeError):\n   964→        return []\n   965→\n   966→    # Scan all deviation records\n   967→    all_records = scan_accepted_deviation_records(config.output_dir)\n   968→    if not all_records:\n   969→        return []\n   970→\n   971→    # Filter to records written AFTER spec-fidelity started (strict >)\n   972→    qualifying = [r for r in all_records if r.mtime > started_at_ts]\n   973→    return qualifying\n   974→\n   975→\n   976→def _apply_resume_after_spec_patch(\n   977→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n   978→    results: list[StepResult],\n   979→    auto_accept: bool,\n   980→    initial_spec_hash: str,\n   981→    cycle_count: int,\n   982→) -> bool:\n   983→    \"\"\"Attempt a single spec-patch auto-resume cycle after spec-fidelity FAIL.\n   984→\n   985→    Evaluates the three-condition detection gate (FR-2.24.1.9):\n   986→      1. Recursion guard: cycle_count == 0\n   987→      2. Qualifying deviation files exist with mtime > started_at\n   988→      3. Spec file hash changed since run started (initial_spec_hash)\n   989→\n   990→    If all conditions pass, executes the six-step disk-reread sequence\n   991→    (FR-2.24.1.10) and re-runs the pipeline via _apply_resume.\n   992→\n   993→    Single-writer assumption: no concurrent writer modifies\n   994→    .roadmap-state.json between the reread and write steps.\n   995→\n   996→    Returns True if the cycle was attempted (regardless of outcome),\n   997→    False if conditions were not met.\n   998→    \"\"\"\n   999→    # FR-2.24.1.11: Recursion guard\n  1000→    if cycle_count >= 1:\n  1001→        print(\n  1002→            \"[roadmap] Spec-patch cycle already exhausted \"\n  1003→            f\"(cycle_count={cycle_count}). Proceeding to normal failure.\",\n  1004→            flush=True,\n  1005→        )\n  1006→        return False\n  1007→\n  1008→    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 2: Qualifying deviation files\n  1009→    qualifying = _find_qualifying_deviation_files(config, results)\n  1010→    if not qualifying:\n  1011→        return False\n  1012→\n  1013→    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 3: Spec hash changed since run started\n  1014→    current_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n  1015→    if current_hash == initial_spec_hash:\n  1016→        return False\n  1017→\n  1018→    # All three conditions met — enter the cycle\n  1019→    # FR-2.24.1.12: Cycle entry logging\n  1020→    print(\n  1021→        f\"[roadmap] Spec patched by subprocess. \"\n  1022→        f\"Found {len(qualifying)} accepted deviation record(s).\",\n  1023→        flush=True,\n  1024→    )\n  1025→    print(\n  1026→        \"[roadmap] Triggering spec-hash sync and resume (cycle 1/1).\",\n  1027→        flush=True,\n  1028→    )\n  1029→\n  1030→    # FR-2.24.1.10: Six-step disk-reread sequence\n  1031→    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n  1032→\n  1033→    # Step 1: Re-read state from disk\n  1034→    _fresh_state = read_state(state_file)  # noqa: F841\n  1035→\n  1036→    # Step 2: Recompute spec hash\n  1037→    new_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n  1038→\n  1039→    # Step 3: Atomic write of new hash\n  1040→    try:\n  1041→        # Read again for fresh copy, update only spec_hash, write atomically\n  1042→        fresh_for_write = read_state(state_file) or {}\n  1043→        fresh_for_write[\"spec_hash\"] = new_hash\n  1044→        write_state(fresh_for_write, state_file)\n  1045→    except OSError as exc:\n  1046→        print(\n  1047→            f\"[roadmap] ERROR: Failed to update spec_hash during \"\n  1048→            f\"auto-resume cycle: {exc}. Falling through to normal failure.\",\n  1049→            file=sys.stderr,\n  1050→            flush=True,\n  1051→        )\n  1052→        return True  # Cycle was attempted but failed — don't retry\n  1053→\n  1054→    # Step 4: Re-read state from disk AGAIN (this is what _apply_resume gets)\n  1055→    post_write_state = read_state(state_file)\n  1056→    if post_write_state is None:\n  1057→        print(\n  1058→            \"[roadmap] ERROR: Could not re-read state after write. \"\n  1059→            \"Falling through to normal failure.\",\n  1060→            file=sys.stderr,\n  1061→            flush=True,\n  1062→        )\n  1063→        return True\n  1064→\n  1065→    # Step 5: Rebuild steps\n  1066→    steps = _build_steps(config)\n  1067→\n  1068→    # Step 6: Apply resume with post-write state\n  1069→    from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n  1070→\n  1071→    steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n  1072→\n  1073→    # Re-execute pipeline from the resumed point\n  1074→    resumed_results = execute_pipeline(\n  1075→        steps=steps,\n  1076→        config=config,\n  1077→        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n  1078→        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n  1079→        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n  1080→    )\n  1081→\n  1082→    # Save state from resumed run\n  1083→    _save_state(config, resumed_results)\n  1084→\n  1085→    # FR-2.24.1.12: Cycle completion logging\n  1086→    print(\"[roadmap] Spec-patch resume cycle complete.\", flush=True)\n  1087→\n  1088→    # Check if resumed pipeline also failed\n  1089→    resumed_failures = [\n  1090→        r for r in resumed_results\n  1091→        if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)\n  1092→    ]\n  1093→    if resumed_failures:\n  1094→        # FR-2.24.1.13: Normal failure on cycle exhaustion\n  1095→        # Use second-run results only\n  1096→        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(resumed_results, config)\n  1097→        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n  1098→        sys.exit(1)\n  1099→\n  1100→    # Proceeding to normal failure.\",\n            flush=True,\n        )\n        return False\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 2: Qualifying deviation files\n    qualifying = _find_qualifying_deviation_files(config, results)\n    if not qualifying:\n        return False\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 3: Spec hash changed since run started\n    current_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n    if current_hash == initial_spec_hash:\n        return False\n\n    # All three conditions met — enter the cycle\n    # FR-2.24.1.12: Cycle entry logging\n    print(\n        f\"[roadmap] Spec patched by subprocess. \"\n        f\"Found {len(qualifying)} accepted deviation record(s).\",\n        flush=True,\n    )\n    print(\n        \"[roadmap] Triggering spec-hash sync and resume (cycle 1/1).\",\n        flush=True,\n    )\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.10: Six-step disk-reread sequence\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n\n    # Step 1: Re-read state from disk\n    _fresh_state = read_state(state_file)  # noqa: F841\n\n    # Step 2: Recompute spec hash\n    new_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n\n    # Step 3: Atomic write of new hash\n    try:\n        # Read again for fresh copy, update only spec_hash, write atomically\n        fresh_for_write = read_state(state_file) or {}\n        fresh_for_write[\"spec_hash\"] = new_hash\n        write_state(fresh_for_write, state_file)\n    except OSError as exc:\n        print(\n            f\"[roadmap] ERROR: Failed to update spec_hash during \"\n            f\"auto-resume cycle: {exc}. Falling through to normal failure.\",\n            file=sys.stderr,\n            flush=True,\n        )\n        return True  # Cycle was attempted but failed — don't retry\n\n    # Step 4: Re-read state from disk AGAIN (this is what _apply_resume gets)\n    post_write_state = read_state(state_file)\n    if post_write_state is None:\n        print(\n            \"[roadmap] ERROR: Could not re-read state after write. \"\n            \"Falling through to normal failure.\",\n            file=sys.stderr,\n            flush=True,\n        )\n        return True\n\n    # Re-execute pipeline from the resumed point\n    resumed_results = execute_pipeline(\n        steps=steps,\n        config=config,\n        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n    )\n\n    # Save state from resumed run\n    _save_state(config, resumed_results)\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.12: Cycle completion logging\n    print(\"[roadmap] Spec-patch resume cycle complete.\", flush=True)\n\n    # Check if resumed pipeline also failed\n    resumed_failures = [\n        r for r in resumed_results\n        if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)\n    ]\n    if resumed_failures:\n        # FR-2.24.1.13: Normal failure on cycle exhaustion\n        # Use second-run results only\n        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(resumed_results, config)\n        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # Resumed pipeline succeeded\n    print(\n        f\"\\n[roadmap] Pipeline complete: {len(resumed_results)} steps passed\",\n        flush=True,\n    )\n    return True\n\ndef _save_validation_status(\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    status: str,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Update .roadmap-state.json with validation status.\n\n    Adds or updates the ``validation`` key without modifying existing state.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    config:\n        RoadmapConfig with output_dir.\n    status:\n        One of \"pass\", \"fail\", or \"skipped\".\n    \"\"\"\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n    state = read_state(state_file)\n    if state is None:\n        state = {}\n    state[\"validation\"] = {\n        \"status\": status,\n        \"timestamp\": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),\n    }\n    write_state(state, state_file)\n\n","numLines":200,"startLine":933,"totalLines":1346}}}
